  var $element = $(this);

    $element.waypoint(function(direction)
    {
            history.pushState('', $element.data('title'), $element.data('url'));
            document.title = $element.data('title');
        ga('set', {page:  $element.data('url'), title: $element.data('title')});
        ga('send', 'pageview');
            
    },
    {
        continuous: false,
        offset: '100px'
    });
  
  
})
